Now I have a clear understanding of the pattern. The key points are:\n\n1. The client struct has a `restclient.Interface` field (in this case `clientBase`)\n2. Methods use the interface to call `Get()`, `Post()`, `Put()`, `Delete()`, etc.\n3. These return `*Request` objects\n4. The request is built up using method chaining with methods like:\n   - `AbsPath()` or `Prefix()` for path\n   - `Resource()` for the resource name\n   - `Namespace()` for namespaced resources\n   - `Name()` for specific resource names\n   - `SubResource()` for subresources\n   - `Body()` for request body\n   - `SpecificallyVersionedParams()` for parameters\n5. `Do(ctx)` executes the request and returns a `Result`\n6. `Result.Error()` checks for errors\n7.
